343    public void initialize() throws Exception
344    {
345        try
346        {
347            initializeSessionManagerInterfaces();
348            initializeSessionManagerV2Interfaces();
349            initializeSessionManagerV3Interfaces();
350            initializeSessionManagerV5Interfaces();
351            initializeSessionManagerV6Interfaces();
352            initializeSessionManagerV7Interfaces();
353            initializeSessionManagerV9Interfaces();
354            
355            eventChannel = EventChannelAdapterFactory.find();
356            eventChannel.setDynamicChannels(true);
357            eventChannel.setListenerCleanup(CommonTranslatorProperties.isCleanChannelAdapterEnabled());
358 
359            initializeCallbackConsumers();
360            initializeCallbackV2Consumers();
361            initializeCallbackV3Consumers();
362 
363            initializeCaches();
364            initializeCachesV2();
365            initializeCachesV3();
366        }
367        catch(Exception e)
368        {
369            GUILoggerHome.find().exception(TRANSLATOR_NAME + ": TraderAPIImpl.initialize", e);
370            throw e;
371        }
372    }
373

375    {
376        initializeSessionlessProductCache();
377        initializeSessionProductCache();
378        initializeOrderCache();
379    }

393        orderEntry = sessionManager.getOrderEntry();
394        tradingSession = sessionManager.getTradingSession();
395        userPreferenceQuery = sessionManager.getUserPreferenceQuery();
396        userHistory = sessionManager.getUserHistory();
397

399    }

447    protected void initializeOrderCache() throws Exception {
448        try {
449            //Create and register these caches with the IEC
450            ChannelKey key;
451 
452            //Register the Caches directly with the IEC
453            orderQueryCache = new OrderQueryCacheProxy();
454            key = new ChannelKey(ChannelType.CB_ALL_ORDERS, new Integer(0));
455            EventChannelAdapterFactory.find().addChannelListener(EventChannelAdapterFactory.find(), orderQueryCache, key);
456 
457            orderBookManager = new TradersOrderBookManager();
458            EventChannelAdapterFactory.find().addChannelListener(EventChannelAdapterFactory.find(), orderBookManager, key);
459 
460            filledReportCache = new FilledReportCache();
461            key = new ChannelKey(ChannelType.CB_FILLED_REPORT, new Integer(0));
462            EventChannelAdapterFactory.find().addChannelListener(EventChannelAdapterFactory.find(), filledReportCache, key);
463 
464            key = new ChannelKey(ChannelType.CB_QUOTE_FILLED_REPORT, new Integer(0));
465            EventChannelAdapterFactory.find().addChannelListener(EventChannelAdapterFactory.find(), filledReportCache, key);
466 
467            bustReportCache = new BustReportCache();
468            key = new ChannelKey(ChannelType.CB_ORDER_BUST_REPORT, new Integer(0));
469            EventChannelAdapterFactory.find().addChannelListener(EventChannelAdapterFactory.find(), bustReportCache, key);
470        } catch (Exception e) {
471 
472            GUILoggerHome.find().exception(TRANSLATOR_NAME+": initializeOrderCache()","",e);
473            throw e;
474        }
475    }
476 
477    protected void initializeSessionlessProductCache() throws Exception
478    {
479        try
480        {
481            ProductType[] productTypes = getAllProductTypes();
482            for(int i = 0 ; i<productTypes.length; i++)
483            {
484                getAllClassesForType(productTypes[i].getType());
485            }
486        }
487        catch(Exception e)
488        {
489            GUILoggerHome.find().exception(TRANSLATOR_NAME+": .initializeSessionlessProductCache()","",e);
490        }
491    }
492 
493    protected void initializeSessionProductCache() throws Exception
494    {
495        try {
496            tradingSessionCache = new TradingSessionCache();
497            TradingSessionStruct[] sessions = getCurrentTradingSessions(tradingSessionCache);
498            tradingSessionCache.addTradingSessions(sessions);
499 
500            for (int i = 0; i < sessions.length; i++) {
501               initializeProductCache(sessions[i].sessionName);
502               productProcessor.subscribeForSessionProductEvents(sessions[i].sessionName);
503               BookDepthProcessor bookDepthProcessor = new BookDepthProcessor(sessions[i].sessionName);
504               bookDepthProcessor.subscribeForBookDepthEvents(sessions[i].sessionName);
505            }
506        } catch (Exception e) {
507            GUILoggerHome.find().exception(TRANSLATOR_NAME+": .initializeSessionCache()","",e);
508            throw e;
509        }
510    }
511 
512    protected void initializeSessionCaches(String sessionName)
513    {
514        initializeProductCache(sessionName);
515    }
516 
517    protected void initializeProductCache(String sessionName)
518    {
519        try
520        {
521            ProductType[] productTypes = getProductTypesForSession(sessionName);
522            for ( int i = 0; i < productTypes.length; i++ ) {
523                  loadProductClassesForSession(sessionName, productTypes[i].getType());
524            }
525        }
526        catch (Exception e)
527        {
528            GUILoggerHome.find().exception(TRANSLATOR_NAME+": .initializeProductCache()","",e);
529        }
530    }
531 
532    protected void initializeCallbackConsumers()
533    {
534        // create the CMICallback consumer cache factory for the eventChannel
535        //  -- CurrentMarket, NBBO, Recap, and BookDepth consumers will be cached by Session/ProductClass
536        cmiConsumerCacheFactory = new CMICallbackConsumerCacheFactoryImpl(eventChannel);
537        // Create all the CMICallback objects
538 
539        expectedOpeningPriceConsumer = ExpectedOpeningPriceConsumerFactory.create(eventChannel);
540        orderStatusConsumer = OrderStatusConsumerFactory.create(eventChannel);
541        classStatusConsumer = ClassStatusConsumerFactory.create(eventChannel);
542        productStatusConsumer = ProductStatusConsumerFactory.create(eventChannel);
543        strategyStatusConsumer = StrategyStatusConsumerFactory.create(eventChannel);
544        tradingSessionStatusConsumer = TradingSessionStatusConsumerFactory.create(eventChannel);
545        tickerConsumer = TickerConsumerFactory.create(eventChannel);
546    }
547 
548    protected void initializeCallbackV2Consumers()
549    {
550        // create the CMICallback consumer cache factory for the eventChannel
551        //  -- CurrentMarket, NBBO, Recap, and BookDepth consumers will be cached by Session/ProductClass
552        cmiConsumerCacheFactoryV2 = new CMICallbackV2ConsumerCacheFactoryImpl(eventChannel);
553 
554        // Create V2 callback consumers
555        //     orderBookConsumerV2 = OrderBookV2ConsumerFactory.create(eventChannel);
556        orderBookUpdateConsumerV2 = OrderBookUpdateV2ConsumerFactory.create(eventChannel);
557        orderStatusConsumerV2 = OrderStatusV2ConsumerFactory.create(eventChannel);
558        tickerConsumerV2 = TickerV2ConsumerFactory.create(eventChannel);
559        
560        quoteStatusConsumerV2 = QuoteStatusV2ConsumerFactory.create(eventChannel);
561    }
562 
563    protected void initializeCallbackV3Consumers()
564    {
565        cmiConsumerCacheFactoryV3 = new CMICallbackV3ConsumerCacheFactoryImpl(eventChannel);
566 
567        // Auction/RFP Consumer or
568        auctionConsumer = AuctionConsumerFactory.create(eventChannel);
569    }

576     */

581        cleanupCachesV3();
582 
583        cleanupCallbackV2Consumers();
584        cleanupCallbackConsumers();
585        cleanupCallbackV3Consumers();
586 
587        cleanupSessionManagerV2Interfaces();
588        cleanupSessionManagerInterfaces();
589        cleanupSessionManagerV3Interfaces();
590 
591        eventChannel = null;
592    }

679    /**
680     * cleanupSessionCache()
681     * @description This method cleans up all user/sessiom related caches
682     * @param       none
683     * @returns     void
684     */
685    private void cleanupSessionCache()
686    {
687        try
688        {
689            TradingSessionStruct[] sessions = tradingSessionCache.getCurrentTradingSessions();
690            for (int i = 0; i < sessions.length; i++)
691            {
692                cleanupProductCache(sessions[ i ].sessionName);
693                sessions[ i ] = null;
694            }
695            unsubscribeTradingSessionStatus(tradingSessionCache);
696            tradingSessionCache = null;
697        }
698        catch (Exception e)
699        {
700            GUILoggerHome.find().exception(TRANSLATOR_NAME+": cleanupSessionCache()","",e);
701        }
702    }

715     * When all listeners have unsubscribed from the internal eventChannel, cleanUp and unsubscribe the UserMarketDataCache from the CAS.

728    /**
729     * cleanupOrderCache()
730     * @description This method cleans up users orders cache object(s)
731     * @param       none
732     * @returns     void
733     */
734    private void cleanupOrderCache()
735    {
736        try {
737            //Create and register these caches with the IEC
738            ChannelKey key;
739 
740            //Un - register the Caches directly with the IEC
741            key = new ChannelKey(ChannelType.CB_ALL_ORDERS, new Integer(0));
742            EventChannelAdapterFactory.find().removeChannelListener(EventChannelAdapterFactory.find(), orderQueryCache, key);
743 
744            EventChannelAdapterFactory.find().removeChannelListener(EventChannelAdapterFactory.find(), orderBookManager, key);
745 
746            key = new ChannelKey(ChannelType.CB_FILLED_REPORT, new Integer(0));
747            EventChannelAdapterFactory.find().removeChannelListener(EventChannelAdapterFactory.find(), filledReportCache, key);
748 
749            key = new ChannelKey(ChannelType.CB_ORDER_BUST_REPORT, new Integer(0));
750            EventChannelAdapterFactory.find().removeChannelListener(EventChannelAdapterFactory.find(), bustReportCache, key);
751 
752            // these 2 may cause corba comm failures because the CAS will unsubscribe them for me
753            // but it may have a time delay and events may come in an attempt to update each cache.
754            orderQueryCache     = null;
755            orderBookManager    = null;
756 
757            filledReportCache   = null;
758            bustReportCache     = null;
759 
760        } catch (Exception e) {
761            GUILoggerHome.find().exception(TRANSLATOR_NAME+": cleanupOrderCache()","",e);
762        }
763    }

791     * @exception CommunicationException

793     * @exception DataValidationException
794     * @retutn UserMarketDataStruct[] Array of UserMarketDataStruct objects
795     */
796    public UserMarketDataStruct[] getUserMarketData(String sessionName, int classKey, EventChannelListener clientListener)
797           throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException
798    {
799        if (GUILoggerHome.find().isDebugOn()&& GUILoggerHome.find().isPropertyOn(GUILoggerBusinessProperty.MARKET_QUERY))
800        {
801            Object[] argObj = new Object[3];
802            argObj[0] = sessionName;
803            argObj[1] = new Integer(classKey);
804            argObj[2] = clientListener;
805 
806            GUILoggerHome.find().debug(TRANSLATOR_NAME+": getUserMarketData",GUILoggerBusinessProperty.MARKET_QUERY,argObj);
807        }
808 
809        // don't allow null listener

811        {
812            throw new IllegalArgumentException(TRANSLATOR_NAME+".getUserMarketData() -- EventChannelListener can't be null");
813        }

815        ChannelKey key = new ChannelKey(ChannelType.CB_USER_MARKET_DATA,  new SessionKeyContainer(sessionName, classKey));
816        // this subscription was moved to addUserMarketDataListener
817        //eventChannel.addChannelListener(EventChannelAdapterFactory.find(), clientListener, key);
818        addUserMarketDataListener(clientListener, key, sessionName, classKey);
819 
820        return getUserMarketDataCacheProxy(sessionName).getUserMarketDataForClass(classKey);
821    }

832     * @retutn UserMarketDataStruct
833     */
834    public UserMarketDataStruct getUserMarketDataByProduct( String sessionName, int productKey, EventChannelListener clientListener )
835           throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException, NotFoundException
836    {
837        if (GUILoggerHome.find().isDebugOn() && GUILoggerHome.find().isPropertyOn(GUILoggerBusinessProperty.MARKET_QUERY))
838        {
839            Object[] argObj = new Object[3];
840            argObj[0] = sessionName;
841            argObj[1] = new Integer(productKey);
842            argObj[2] = clientListener;

844            GUILoggerHome.find().debug(TRANSLATOR_NAME+": getUserMarketDataByProduct",GUILoggerBusinessProperty.MARKET_QUERY,argObj);

848

850        if (clientListener != null) {
851            ChannelKey key = new ChannelKey(ChannelType.CB_USER_MARKET_DATA_BY_PRODUCT, productKeyObj);

853            //eventChannel.addChannelListener(EventChannelAdapterFactory.find(), clientListener, key);
854

856            addUserMarketDataListener(clientListener, key, sessionName, classKey);

860    }

864     * for the given product key.
865     *
866     * @param productKey the product key to unsubscribe for
867     * @param clientListener the client listener to unsubscribe from receiving data
868     * @exception SystemException
869     * @exception CommunicationException
870     * @exception AuthorizationException
871     * @exception DataValidationException
872     * @exception NotFoundException
873     */
874    public void unsubscribeUserMarketDataByProduct(String sessionName, int productKey, EventChannelListener clientListener)
875            throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException, NotFoundException
876    {
877        if(GUILoggerHome.find().isDebugOn() &&
878           GUILoggerHome.find().isPropertyOn(GUILoggerBusinessProperty.MARKET_QUERY))
879        {
880            Object[] argObj = new Object[3];
881            argObj[0] = sessionName;
882            argObj[1] = productKey;
883            argObj[2] = clientListener;
884 
885            GUILoggerHome.find().debug(TRANSLATOR_NAME + ": unsubscribeUserMarketDataByProduct",
886                                       GUILoggerBusinessProperty.MARKET_QUERY, argObj);
887        }
888 
889        if(clientListener != null)
890        {
891            ChannelKey key = new ChannelKey(ChannelType.CB_USER_MARKET_DATA_BY_PRODUCT, new SessionKeyContainer(sessionName, productKey));
892            // this will remove the eventChannel listener and decrement the listener count for the Session/Class

894        }
895    }

1006    /**
1007     * Gets order detail information from an order id.
1008     *
1009     * @return OderDetailStruct
1010     *
1011     * @param orderId the order id to query for.
1012     * @param cacheOnly if true only tries to find the order in the local order cache
1013     *
1014     * @exception SystemException
1015     * @exception CommunicationException
1016     * @exception AuthorizationException
1017     * @exception DataValidationException
1018     * @exception NotFoundException
1019     */
1020    public OrderDetailStruct getOrderById(OrderIdStruct orderId, final boolean cacheOnly)
1021    throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException, NotFoundException
1022    {
1023        OrderDetailStruct order = null;
1024 
1025        if (GUILoggerHome.find().isDebugOn() && GUILoggerHome.find().isPropertyOn(GUILoggerBusinessProperty.ORDER_QUERY))
1026        {
1027            GUILoggerHome.find().debug(TRANSLATOR_NAME+": getOrderById",GUILoggerBusinessProperty.ORDER_QUERY,orderId);
1028        }
1029 
1030        if(cacheOnly)
1031        {
1032            order = orderQueryCache.getOrderById(orderId);
1033        }
1034        else if (isOmtRole())
1035        {
1036            OrderStruct struct = APIHome.findOrderManagementTerminalAPI().getOrderByIdV2(orderId);
1037            if(struct != null)
1038            {
1039                order = buildOrderDetailStruct(struct);
1040            }
1041        }
1042        else
1043        {
1044        order = orderQueryCache.getOrderById(orderId);
1045            if ( order == null )
1046            {
1047           order = orderQuery.getOrderById(orderId);
1048            }
1049           orderQueryCache.addOrder(order);
1050        }
1051        return order;
1052    }

1282    /**
1283     * A convenience method to get all SessionProductClass'es for all product types.
1284     * @param sessionName to get all classes for all types
1285     * @return and array of SessionProductClass that are contained by passed sessionName for all product types
1286     */
1287    public SessionProductClass[] getAllProductClassesForSession(String sessionName)
1288            throws SystemException, DataValidationException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException
1289    {
1290        SessionProductClass[] spc;
1291 
1292        ProductType[] allTypes = getProductTypesForSession(sessionName);
1293        List<SessionProductClass> allSPCs = new ArrayList<SessionProductClass>(allTypes.length * 200);
1294 
1295        for(int i = 0; i < allTypes.length; i++)
1296        {
1297            ProductType productType = allTypes[i];
1298            spc = getProductClassesForSession(sessionName, productType.getType(), null);
1299            for(int j = 0; j < spc.length; j++)
1300            {
1301                SessionProductClass sessionProductClass = spc[j];
1302                allSPCs.add(sessionProductClass);
1303            }
1304        }
1305 
1306        spc = new SessionProductClass[allSPCs.size()];
1307        spc = (SessionProductClass[]) allSPCs.toArray(spc);
1308 
1309        return spc;
1310    }

1374    /*
1375     * subscribe all products for the given product class and registers a client-side
1376     * callback listener to receive further products of the given class.
1377     *
1378     * @param classKey the product class key to get product information for.
1379     * @param includeActiveOnly true to receive active products only, false to receive all products.
1380     * @param clientListener the subscribing listener.
1381     */
1382    public void subscribeProductsForSession(String sessionName, int classKey, EventChannelListener clientListener)
1383           throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException
1384    {
1385        try {
1386            ChannelKey key = new ChannelKey(ChannelType.CB_PRODUCT_STATE_BY_CLASS, new SessionKeyContainer(sessionName,classKey));
1387            SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().subscribe(key, clientListener, productStatusConsumer);
1388            key = new ChannelKey(ChannelType.CB_PRODUCT_UPDATE_BY_CLASS, new SessionKeyContainer(sessionName, classKey));
1389            SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().subscribe(key, clientListener, productStatusConsumer);
1390            if ( isStrategy(classKey) ){
1391                getStrategiesByClassForSession(sessionName, classKey, clientListener);
1392                return;
1393            }
1394            loadProductsForClassBySession(sessionName, classKey);
1395        } catch (NotFoundException e) {
1396            DataValidationException de = new DataValidationException();
1397            de.details = e.details;
1398            throw de;
1399        }
1400    }
1401 
1402    /*
1403     * subscribe all products for the given product class and registers a client-side
1404     * callback listener to receive further products of the given class.
1405     *
1406     * @param classKey the product class key to get product information for.
1407     * @param includeActiveOnly true to receive active products only, false to receive all products.
1408     * @param clientListener the subscribing listener.
1409     * vista
1410     */
1411    public void subscribeSessionClassByType(String sessionName, short productType, EventChannelListener clientListener)
1412           throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException
1413    {
1414        ChannelKey key1 = new ChannelKey(ChannelType.CB_CLASS_UPDATE_BY_TYPE, new SessionKeyContainer(sessionName, productType));
1415        int subscriptionCount1 = SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().subscribe(key1, clientListener, classStatusConsumer);
1416        ChannelKey key2 = new ChannelKey(ChannelType.CB_CLASS_STATE_BY_TYPE, new SessionKeyContainer(sessionName, productType));
1417        int subscriptionCount2 = SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().subscribe(key2, clientListener, classStatusConsumer);
1418        if ( subscriptionCount1 == 1 && subscriptionCount2 == 1 ) {
1419            try
1420            {
1421                loadProductClassesForSession(sessionName, productType);
1422            }
1423            catch (SystemException e)
1424            {
1425                SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().unsubscribe(key1, clientListener, classStatusConsumer);
1426                SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().unsubscribe(key2, clientListener, classStatusConsumer);
1427                throw e;
1428            }
1429            catch (CommunicationException e)
1430            {
1431                SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().unsubscribe(key1, clientListener, classStatusConsumer);
1432                SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().unsubscribe(key2, clientListener, classStatusConsumer);
1433                throw e;
1434            }
1435            catch (AuthorizationException e)
1436            {
1437                SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().unsubscribe(key1, clientListener, classStatusConsumer);
1438                SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().unsubscribe(key2, clientListener, classStatusConsumer);
1439                throw e;
1440            }
1441            catch (DataValidationException e)
1442            {
1443                SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().unsubscribe(key1, clientListener, classStatusConsumer);
1444                SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().unsubscribe(key2, clientListener, classStatusConsumer);
1445                throw e;
1446            }
1447        }
1448    }

1450    /**
1451     * Gets product information for a given product by its name.  If there is a product miss, load all the products in this class
1452     *
1453     * @author Derek T. Chambers-Boucher
1454     *
1455     * @return a ProductStruct containing information about the given product.
1456     * @param productName the name of the product.
1457     * @exception SystemException
1458     * @exception CommunicationException
1459     * @exception AuthorizationException
1460     * @exception DataValidationException
1461     * @author Jing Chen
1462     * @version 08/07/01
1463     *
1464     */
1465    public Product getProductByName(ProductNameStruct productName)
1466           throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException, NotFoundException
1467    {
1468        Product product = ProductQueryCacheFactory.find().getProductByName(productName);
1469        // Cache miss. Retrieve it via cmi and reload products for that class
1470        if ( product == null ) {
1471            if (GUILoggerHome.find().isDebugOn() && GUILoggerHome.find().isPropertyOn(GUILoggerBusinessProperty.PRODUCT_QUERY))
1472            {
1473                GUILoggerHome.find().debug(TRANSLATOR_NAME + ": getProductByName calling productQuery.getProductByName()", GUILoggerBusinessProperty.PRODUCT_QUERY, productName);
1474            }
1475            ProductStruct productStruct = productQuery.getProductByName(productName);
1476            if (productStruct.productKeys.productType == ProductTypes.STRATEGY) {
1477                if (GUILoggerHome.find().isDebugOn() && GUILoggerHome.find().isPropertyOn(GUILoggerBusinessProperty.PRODUCT_QUERY))
1478                {
1479                    GUILoggerHome.find().debug(TRANSLATOR_NAME + ": getProductByName calling productQuery.getStrategyByKey()", GUILoggerBusinessProperty.PRODUCT_QUERY, productStruct.productKeys.productKey);
1480                }
1481                StrategyStruct strategyStruct= productQuery.getStrategyByKey(productStruct.productKeys.productKey);
1482                ProductQueryCacheFactory.find().updateStrategy(ProductFactoryHome.find().create(strategyStruct));
1483                //loadStrategiesForClass(productStruct.productKeys.classKey);
1484                product = ProductQueryCacheFactory.find().getStrategyByName(productName);
1485            } else {
1486                ProductQueryCacheFactory.find().updateProduct(ProductFactoryHome.find().create(productStruct));
1487                //loadProductsForClass(productStruct.productKeys.classKey);
1488                product = ProductQueryCacheFactory.find().getProductByName(productName);
1489            }
1490            if (product == null)
1491            {
1492                 throw ExceptionBuilder.notFoundException("No product found with productName = " + productName + " in translator product cache", 0);
1493            }
1494        }
1495        return product;
1496    }

1616        {
1617            reportingClass = getReportingClassBySymbol(reportingClassSymbol);
1618        }
1619        catch (NotFoundException e)
1620        {
1621            throw e;
1622        }
1623 
1624        Product[] products = null;
1625        try
1626        {
1627            products = getProductsForReportingClass(reportingClass, false);
1628        }
1629        catch (UserException e)
1630        {
1631            throw e;
1632        }
1633 
1634        if (products != null)
1635        {
1636            for (int p=0; p<products.length; p++)
1637            {
1638                char pMonthCode = products[p].getOpraMonthCode();
1639                char pPriceCode = products[p].getOpraPriceCode();
1640                if (pMonthCode == monthCode && pPriceCode == priceCode)
1641                {
1642                    return products[p];
1643                }
1644            }
1645        }
1646 
1647        return null;
1648    }
1649 
1650    /**
1651     * Gets the session reporting class with the passed key for the passed session
1652     * @param reportingClassKey to get reporting class for
1653     * @param sessionName to get reporting class for
1654     * @return reporting class with matching key
1655     * @exception NotFoundException a reporting class with the passed key could not be found
1656     * @exception DataValidationException the passed sessionName was invalid
1657     */
1658    public SessionReportingClass getReportingClassByKeyForSession(int reportingClassKey, String sessionName)
1659            throws NotFoundException, DataValidationException
1660    {
1661        SessionReportingClass reportingClass = null;
1662 
1663        TradingSessionStruct[] sessions = tradingSessionCache.getCurrentTradingSessions();
1664        boolean foundSession = false;
1665        for(int i = 0; i < sessions.length; i++)
1666        {
1667            if(sessions[i].sessionName.equals(sessionName))
1668            {
1669                foundSession = true;
1670                break;
1671            }
1672        }
1673 
1674        if(!foundSession)
1675        {
1676            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("Session name was not a valid session:" + sessionName,
1677                                                           DataValidationCodes.INVALID_SESSION);
1678        }
1679 
1680        reportingClass = SessionProductCacheFactory.find(sessionName).getReportingClassByKey(reportingClassKey);
1681 
1682        if(reportingClass == null)
1683        {
1684            throw ExceptionBuilder.notFoundException("Reporting Class does not exist:" + reportingClassKey +
1685                                                     ", for session:" + sessionName,
1686                                                     NotFoundCodes.RESOURCE_DOESNT_EXIST);
1687        }
1688 
1689        return reportingClass;
1690 
1691    }

1725    /**
1726     * Gets a product class by key.
1727     *
1728     * @param classKey the class
1729     * @exception SystemException
1730     * @exception CommunicationException
1731     * @exception AuthorizationException
1732     * @exception DataValidationException
1733     * @exception NotFoundException
1734     * @return the product class struct.
1735     */
1736    public ProductClass getProductClassByKey(int classKey)
1737           throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException, NotFoundException {
1738 
1739        ProductClass productClass = null;
1740 
1741        if(classKey == DEFAULT_CLASS_KEY)
1742        {
1743            productClass = getDefaultProductClass();
1744        }
1745        else if(classKey == ALL_SELECTED_CLASS_KEY)
1746        {
1747            productClass = getAllSelectedProductClass();
1748        }
1749        else
1750        {
1751            productClass = ProductQueryCacheFactory.find().getProductClassByKey(classKey);
1752        }
1753 
1754        if(productClass == null)
1755        {
1756            if (GUILoggerHome.find().isDebugOn() && GUILoggerHome.find().isPropertyOn(GUILoggerBusinessProperty.PRODUCT_QUERY))
1757            {
1758                GUILoggerHome.find().debug(TRANSLATOR_NAME + ": getProductClassByKey calling productQuery.getClassByKey()", GUILoggerBusinessProperty.PRODUCT_QUERY, classKey);
1759            }
1760            ClassStruct rawClass = productQuery.getClassByKey(classKey);
1761            ProductClass rawProductClass = ProductClassFactoryHome.find().create(rawClass);
1762            ProductQueryCacheFactory.find().addClass(rawProductClass, rawProductClass.getProductType());
1763            productClass = ProductQueryCacheFactory.find().getProductClassByKey(classKey);
1764        }
1765 
1766        return productClass;
1767    }

1769    /**
1770     * gets class by sessionName and classKey.
1771     * @param sessionName   String
1772     * @param classKey      int
1773     * @return SessionProductClass
1774     * @exception SystemException
1775     * @exception CommunicationException
1776     * @exception AuthorizationException
1777     * @exception DataValidationException
1778     * @exception NotFoundException
1779     */
1780    public SessionProductClass getClassByKeyForSession(String sessionName, int classKey)
1781           throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException, NotFoundException
1782    {
1783        SessionProductClass sessionProductClass = null;
1784 
1785        if(classKey == DEFAULT_CLASS_KEY)
1786        {
1787            sessionProductClass = getDefaultSessionProductClass(sessionName);
1788        }
1789        else if(classKey == ALL_SELECTED_CLASS_KEY)
1790        {
1791            sessionProductClass = getAllSelectedSessionProductClass(sessionName);
1792        }
1793        else if(sessionName.equals(DefaultTradingSession.DEFAULT))
1794        {
1795            ProductClass productClass = getProductClassByKey(classKey);
1796            sessionProductClass = SessionProductClassFactory.create(sessionName,  productClass);
1797        }
1798        else
1799        {
1800            //attempts to find the product from cache
1801            sessionProductClass = SessionProductCacheFactory.find(sessionName).getClassByKey(classKey);
1802        }
1803 
1804        // if not found, calls CAS tradingSession to get class and stores it at the cache
1805        if (sessionProductClass == null)
1806        {
1807            Object[] argObj = new Object[]{sessionName, classKey};
1808            if (GUILoggerHome.find().isDebugOn() && GUILoggerHome.find().isPropertyOn(GUILoggerBusinessProperty.PRODUCT_QUERY))
1809            {
1810                GUILoggerHome.find().debug(TRANSLATOR_NAME + ": getClassByKeyForSession calling tradingSession.getClassBySessionForKey()", GUILoggerBusinessProperty.PRODUCT_QUERY, argObj);
1811            }
1812            SessionClassStruct sessionClassStruct = tradingSession.getClassBySessionForKey(sessionName, classKey);
1813            sessionProductClass = SessionProductClassFactory.create(sessionClassStruct);
1814            ProductClass productClass = ProductClassFactoryHome.find().create(sessionClassStruct.classStruct);
1815            ProductQueryCacheFactory.find().addClass(productClass, sessionClassStruct.classStruct.productType);
1816            productProcessor.addClass(sessionClassStruct);
1817        }
1818 
1819        return sessionProductClass;
1820    }
1821 
1822    /**
1823     * Gets the session product by productKey.  It looks into the cache first.  If not found
1824     * in cache, call CAS TradingSession to get it and store it in cache
1825     * @param sessionName     String
1826     * @param productKey      int
1827     * @return SessionProduct
1828     * @exception SystemException
1829     * @exception CommunicationException
1830     * @exception AuthorizationException
1831     * @exception DataValidationException
1832     * @exception NotFoundException
1833     */
1834    public SessionProduct getProductByKeyForSession(String sessionName, int productKey)
1835           throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException, NotFoundException
1836    {
1837        SessionProduct sessionProduct = null;
1838        if(productKey == DEFAULT_PRODUCT_KEY)
1839        {
1840            sessionProduct = getDefaultSessionProduct(sessionName);
1841        }
1842        else if(productKey == DEFAULT_STRATEGY_PRODUCT_KEY)
1843        {
1844            sessionProduct = getDefaultSessionStrategy();
1845        }
1846        else if(productKey == ALL_SELECTED_PRODUCT_KEY)
1847        {
1848            sessionProduct = getAllSelectedSessionProduct(sessionName);
1849        }
1850        else
1851        {
1852            // attempts to find it in cache
1853            sessionProduct = SessionProductCacheFactory.find(sessionName).getProductByKey(productKey);
1854            if(sessionProduct == null)
1855            {   // try to find in inactive session products cache
1856                sessionProduct = SessionProductCacheFactory.find(SessionProduct.NOT_IN_TRADING_SESSION).getProductByKey(productKey);
1857            }
1858        }
1859        // if not found in cache, call CAS tradingSession to get the product and reload all the products in that class
1860        if (sessionProduct == null)
1861        {
1862            SessionProductStruct sessionProductStruct = null;
1863            try
1864            {
1865                Object[] argObj = new Object[]{sessionName, productKey};
1866                if (GUILoggerHome.find().isDebugOn() && GUILoggerHome.find().isPropertyOn(GUILoggerBusinessProperty.PRODUCT_QUERY))
1867                {
1868                    GUILoggerHome.find().debug(TRANSLATOR_NAME + ": getProductByKeyForSession calling tradingSession.getProductBySessionForKey()", GUILoggerBusinessProperty.PRODUCT_QUERY, argObj);
1869                }
1870                sessionProductStruct = tradingSession.getProductBySessionForKey(sessionName, productKey);
1871                if (sessionProductStruct.productStruct.productKeys.productType == ProductTypes.STRATEGY)
1872                {
1873                    if (GUILoggerHome.find().isDebugOn() && GUILoggerHome.find().isPropertyOn(GUILoggerBusinessProperty.PRODUCT_QUERY))
1874                    {
1875                        GUILoggerHome.find().debug(TRANSLATOR_NAME + ": getProductByKeyForSession calling tradingSession.getStrategyBySessionForKey()", GUILoggerBusinessProperty.PRODUCT_QUERY, argObj);
1876                    }
1877                   SessionStrategyStruct sessionStrategyStruct = tradingSession.getStrategyBySessionForKey(sessionName, productKey);
1878                   productProcessor.updateStrategy(sessionStrategyStruct);
1879                   //loadStrategiesForClassBySession(sessionName, sessionProductStruct.productStruct.productKeys.classKey);
1880                   sessionProduct = SessionProductCacheFactory.find(sessionName).getStrategyByKey(productKey);
1881                } else {
1882                   productProcessor.updateProduct(sessionProductStruct);
1883                   //loadProductsForClassBySession(sessionName, sessionProductStruct.productStruct.productKeys.classKey);
1884                   sessionProduct = SessionProductCacheFactory.find(sessionName).getProductByKey(productKey);
1885                }
1886                // can this ever be reached?? tradingSession.getProductBySessionForKey(sessionName, productKey) would either 
1887                // find and return the product (so the cache would've been updated above), or it would throw an exception
1888                if(sessionProduct == null)
1889                {
1890                    sessionProduct = findInactiveSessionProduct(sessionName, productKey);
1891                }
1892            }
1893            catch(NotFoundException e)
1894            {   // the product is not part of the session, see if we can create an inactive product
1895                sessionProduct = findInactiveSessionProduct(sessionName, productKey);
1896            }
1897            if (sessionProduct == null)
1898            {
1899                throw ExceptionBuilder.notFoundException("No product found with key = " + productKey +" in session:" + sessionName + " in translator product cache", 0);
1900            }
1901        }
1902        return sessionProduct;
1903    }
1904 
1905    protected SessionProduct findInactiveSessionProduct(String sessionName, int productKey)
1906        throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException, NotFoundException
1907    {
1908        SessionProduct sessionProduct = null;
1909        // try to find it in the session cache for inactive session products
1910        sessionProduct = SessionProductCacheFactory.find(SessionProduct.NOT_IN_TRADING_SESSION).getProductByKey(productKey);
1911        if(sessionProduct == null) // not in the cache, so create it
1912        {
1913            // There are two possibilities.  The product does not exist anymore, or the
1914            // product is inactive and consequently out of the session.
1915            // In the second case, we'll create an InactiveSessionProduct to represent the product.
1916 
1917            // need to get the product struct
1918            ProductStruct productStruct = productQuery.getProductByKey(productKey);
1919            // Only create an InactiveSessionProduct for existing inactive products
1920            if(productStruct != null && productStruct.listingState != ListingStates.ACTIVE)
1921            {
1922                // now add inactive product
1923                if (productStruct.productKeys.productType == ProductTypes.STRATEGY)
1924                {
1925                    StrategyStruct strategyStruct = productQuery.getStrategyByKey(productKey);
1926                    sessionProduct = productProcessor.addInactiveSessionStrategy(sessionName, SessionProduct.NOT_IN_TRADING_SESSION, strategyStruct);
1927                }
1928                else
1929                {
1930                    sessionProduct = productProcessor.addInactiveSessionProduct(sessionName, SessionProduct.NOT_IN_TRADING_SESSION, productStruct);
1931                }
1932            }
1933        }
1934        return sessionProduct;
1935    }
1936 
1937 
1938    /**
1939     * Gets the session product by product name.  It looks into the cache first.  If not found
1940     * in cache, call CAS TradingSession to get it and store it in cache
1941     * @param sessionName     String
1942     * @param productName      ProductNameStruct
1943     * @return SessionProduct
1944     * @exception SystemException
1945     * @exception CommunicationException
1946     * @exception AuthorizationException
1947     * @exception DataValidationException
1948     * @exception NotFoundException
1949     */
1950    public SessionProduct getProductByNameForSession(String sessionName, ProductNameStruct productName)
1951        throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException, NotFoundException
1952    {
1953        // attempts to find it in cache
1954        SessionProduct sessionProduct = SessionProductCacheFactory.find(sessionName).getProductByName(productName);
1955        if(sessionProduct == null)
1956        {   // try to find in inactive session products cache
1957            sessionProduct = SessionProductCacheFactory.find(SessionProduct.NOT_IN_TRADING_SESSION).getProductByName(productName);
1958        }
1959        // if not found in cache, call CAS tradingSession to get the product and add the product into the cache
1960        if (sessionProduct == null) {
1961            try
1962            {
1963                Object[] argObj = new Object[]{sessionName, productName};
1964 
1965                if (GUILoggerHome.find().isDebugOn() && GUILoggerHome.find().isPropertyOn(GUILoggerBusinessProperty.PRODUCT_QUERY))
1966                {
1967                    GUILoggerHome.find().debug(TRANSLATOR_NAME + ": getProductByNameForSession calling tradingSession.getProductBySessionForName()", GUILoggerBusinessProperty.PRODUCT_QUERY, argObj);
1968                }
1969 
1970                SessionProductStruct sessionProductStruct = tradingSession.getProductBySessionForName(sessionName, productName);
1971 
1972                if (sessionProductStruct.productStruct.productKeys.productType == ProductTypes.STRATEGY)
1973                {
1974                    if (GUILoggerHome.find().isDebugOn() && GUILoggerHome.find().isPropertyOn(GUILoggerBusinessProperty.PRODUCT_QUERY))
1975                    {
1976                        argObj = new Object[]{sessionName, sessionProductStruct.productStruct.productKeys.productKey};
1977                        GUILoggerHome.find().debug(TRANSLATOR_NAME + ": getProductByNameForSession calling tradingSession.getStrategyBySessionForKey()", GUILoggerBusinessProperty.PRODUCT_QUERY, argObj);
1978                    }
1979                    SessionStrategyStruct sessionStrategyStruct = tradingSession.getStrategyBySessionForKey(sessionName,sessionProductStruct.productStruct.productKeys.productKey);
1980                    productProcessor.updateStrategy(sessionStrategyStruct);
1981                    //loadStrategiesForClassBySession(sessionName, sessionProductStruct.productStruct.productKeys.classKey);
1982                    sessionProduct = SessionProductCacheFactory.find(sessionName).getStrategyByKey(sessionProductStruct.productStruct.productKeys.productKey);
1983                } else {
1984                    productProcessor.updateProduct(sessionProductStruct);
1985                    //loadProductsForClassBySession(sessionName, sessionProductStruct.productStruct.productKeys.classKey);
1986                    sessionProduct = SessionProductCacheFactory.find(sessionName).getProductByKey(sessionProductStruct.productStruct.productKeys.productKey);
1987                }
1988                if(sessionProduct == null)
1989                {
1990                    ProductStruct productStruct = productQuery.getProductByName(productName);
1991                    if( productStruct != null )
1992                    {
1993                        sessionProduct = findInactiveSessionProduct(sessionName, productStruct.productKeys.productKey);
1994                    }
1995                }
1996            }
1997            catch(NotFoundException e)
1998            {   // the product is not part of the session, see if we can create an inactive product
1999                ProductStruct productStruct = productQuery.getProductByName(productName);
2000                if( productStruct != null )
2001                {
2002                    sessionProduct = findInactiveSessionProduct(sessionName, productStruct.productKeys.productKey);
2003                }
2004            }
2005 
2006            if (sessionProduct == null)
2007            {
2008                 throw ExceptionBuilder.notFoundException("No product found with productName = " + productName + " in session = "+ sessionName+" in translator product cache", 0);
2009            }
2010        }
2011        return sessionProduct;
2012    }
2013

2017     * @param sessionName     St

2020     * @param className       String

2056    /**
2057     * Gets a product by key.
2058     *
2059     * @param productKey the product
2060     * @exception SystemException
2061     * @exception CommunicationException
2062     * @exception AuthorizationException
2063     * @exception DataValidationException
2064     * @exception NotFoundException
2065     * @return the product class struct.
2066     */
2067    public Product getProductByKey(int productKey)
2068           throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException, NotFoundException {
2069 
2070        Product product = null;
2071 
2072        if(productKey == DEFAULT_PRODUCT_KEY)
2073        {
2074            product = getDefaultProduct();
2075        }
2076        else if(productKey == ALL_SELECTED_PRODUCT_KEY)
2077        {
2078            product = getAllSelectedProduct();
2079        }
2080        else if(productKey == DEFAULT_STRATEGY_PRODUCT_KEY)
2081        {
2082            product = getDefaultStrategy();
2083        }
2084        else
2085        {
2086            product = ProductQueryCacheFactory.find().getProductByKey(productKey);
2087        }
2088 
2089        if (product == null)
2090        {
2091            if (GUILoggerHome.find().isDebugOn() && GUILoggerHome.find().isPropertyOn(GUILoggerBusinessProperty.PRODUCT_QUERY))
2092            {
2093                GUILoggerHome.find().debug(TRANSLATOR_NAME + ": getProductByKey calling productQuery.getProductByKey()", GUILoggerBusinessProperty.PRODUCT_QUERY, productKey);
2094            }
2095            ProductStruct productStruct = productQuery.getProductByKey(productKey);
2096            if (productStruct.productKeys.productType == ProductTypes.STRATEGY)
2097            {
2098                if (GUILoggerHome.find().isDebugOn() && GUILoggerHome.find().isPropertyOn(GUILoggerBusinessProperty.PRODUCT_QUERY))
2099                {
2100                    GUILoggerHome.find().debug(TRANSLATOR_NAME + ": getProductByKey calling productQuery.getStrategyByKey()", GUILoggerBusinessProperty.PRODUCT_QUERY, productKey);
2101                }
2102                StrategyStruct strategyStruct= productQuery.getStrategyByKey(productKey);
2103                ProductQueryCacheFactory.find().updateStrategy(ProductFactoryHome.find().create(strategyStruct));
2104                //loadStrategiesForClass(productStruct.productKeys.classKey);
2105                product = ProductQueryCacheFactory.find().getStrategyByKey(productKey);
2106            } else {
2107                ProductQueryCacheFactory.find().updateProduct(ProductFactoryHome.find().create(productStruct));
2108                //loadProductsForClass(productStruct.productKeys.classKey);
2109                product = ProductQueryCacheFactory.find().getProductByKey(productKey);
2110            }
2111            if (product == null)
2112            {
2113                throw ExceptionBuilder.notFoundException("No product found with key = " + productKey +" in translator product cache", 0);
2114            }
2115        }
2116        return product;
2117    }

2182    /**
2183     * Gets SessionStrategy by sessionName and productKey.  It looks into the cache first.
2184     * If not found at cache, it calls CAS tradingSession to get the strategy and stores it at the cache
2185     * @param sessionName   String
2186     * @param productKey    int
2187     * @return SessionStrategyContainer
2188     * @exception SystemException
2189     * @exception CommunicationException
2190     * @exception AuthorizationException
2191     * @exception DataValidataionException
2192     */
2193    public SessionStrategy getStrategyByKeyForSession(String sessionName, int productKey)
2194        throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException
2195    {
2196        try {
2197            SessionStrategy sessionStrategy = SessionProductCacheFactory.find(sessionName).getStrategyByKey(productKey);
2198            if(sessionStrategy == null)
2199            {   // try to find in inactive session products cache
2200                sessionStrategy = SessionProductCacheFactory.find(SessionProduct.NOT_IN_TRADING_SESSION).getStrategyByKey(productKey);
2201            }
2202            if (sessionStrategy == null)
2203            {
2204                try
2205                {
2206                    if (GUILoggerHome.find().isDebugOn() && GUILoggerHome.find().isPropertyOn(GUILoggerBusinessProperty.PRODUCT_QUERY))
2207                    {
2208                        Object[] argObj = new Object[2];
2209                        argObj[0] = sessionName;
2210                        argObj[1] = productKey;
2211 
2212                        GUILoggerHome.find().debug(TRANSLATOR_NAME + ": getStrategyByKeyForSession calling tradingSession.getStrategyBySessionForKey()", GUILoggerBusinessProperty.PRODUCT_QUERY, argObj);
2213                    }
2214                    SessionStrategyStruct sessionStrategyStruct = tradingSession.getStrategyBySessionForKey(sessionName, productKey);
2215                    productProcessor.updateStrategy(sessionStrategyStruct);
2216                    //loadStrategiesForClassBySession(sessionName, sessionStrategyStruct.sessionProductStruct.productStruct.productKeys.classKey);
2217                    sessionStrategy = SessionProductCacheFactory.find(sessionName).getStrategyByKey(productKey);
2218                    if( sessionStrategy == null)
2219                    {
2220                        sessionStrategy = (SessionStrategy) findInactiveSessionProduct(sessionName, productKey);
2221                    }
2222                }
2223                catch(NotFoundException e)
2224                {   // the product is not part of the session, see if we can create an inactive product
2225                    sessionStrategy = (SessionStrategy) findInactiveSessionProduct(sessionName, productKey);
2226                }
2227                if (sessionStrategy == null)
2228                {
2229                     throw ExceptionBuilder.notFoundException("No strategy found with productKey = " + productKey + " in session = "+ sessionName+" in translator product cache", 0);
2230                }
2231            }
2232            return sessionStrategy;
2233        } catch (NotFoundException e) {
2234            DataValidationException de = new DataValidationException();
2235            de.details = e.details;
2236            throw de;
2237        }
2238    }

2638    public void subscribeRecapForClass(String sessionName, int classKey, EventChannelListener clientListener)
2639            throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException {
2640 
2641        ChannelKey key = new ChannelKey(ChannelType.CB_RECAP_BY_CLASS, new SessionKeyContainer(sessionName, classKey));
2642 
2643        if (GUILoggerHome.find().isDebugOn() && GUILoggerHome.find().isPropertyOn(GUILoggerBusinessProperty.MARKET_QUERY))
2644        {
2645            Object[] argObj = new Object[3];
2646            argObj[0] = sessionName;
2647            argObj[1] = new Integer(classKey);
2648            argObj[2] = clientListener;
2649 
2650            GUILoggerHome.find().debug(TRANSLATOR_NAME+": subscribeRecapForClass", GUILoggerBusinessProperty.MARKET_QUERY, argObj);
2651        }
2652 
2653        CMIRecapConsumer recapConsumer = cmiConsumerCacheFactory.getRecapConsumerCache().getRecapConsumer(sessionName, classKey);
2654 
2655        if (SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().subscribe(key, clientListener, recapConsumer) == 1) {
2656            GUILoggerHome.find().debug(TRANSLATOR_NAME+": subscribeRecapForClass", GUILoggerBusinessProperty.MARKET_QUERY,"subscribing translator to CAS for Recap for session='"+sessionName+"' classKey="+classKey);
2657            try
2658            {
2659                marketQuery.subscribeRecapForClass(sessionName, classKey, recapConsumer);
2660            }
2661            catch (SystemException e)
2662            {
2663                SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().unsubscribe(key, clientListener, recapConsumer);
2664                throw e;
2665            }
2666            catch (CommunicationException e)
2667            {
2668                SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().unsubscribe(key, clientListener, recapConsumer);
2669                throw e;
2670            }
2671            catch (AuthorizationException e)
2672            {
2673                SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().unsubscribe(key, clientListener, recapConsumer);
2674                throw e;
2675            }
2676            catch (DataValidationException e)
2677            {
2678                SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().unsubscribe(key, clientListener, recapConsumer);
2679                throw e;
2680            }
2681        }
2682    }

2684    public void subscribeRecapForProduct(String sessionName, int productKey, EventChannelListener clientListener)
2685            throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException {
2686 
2687        ChannelKey productChannelKey = new ChannelKey(ChannelType.CB_RECAP_BY_PRODUCT, new SessionKeyContainer(sessionName, productKey));
2688        if (GUILoggerHome.find().isDebugOn() && GUILoggerHome.find().isPropertyOn(GUILoggerBusinessProperty.MARKET_QUERY))
2689        {
2690            Object[] argObj = new Object[3];
2691            argObj[0] = sessionName;
2692            argObj[1] = new Integer(productKey);
2693            argObj[2] = clientListener;
2694 
2695            GUILoggerHome.find().debug(TRANSLATOR_NAME+": subscribeRecapForProduct", GUILoggerBusinessProperty.MARKET_QUERY, argObj);
2696        }
2697 
2698        try
2699        {
2700            // for CurrentMarket by SessionProduct, use the CMICurrentMarketConsumer for the SessionProductClass
2701            int classKey = getProductByKeyForSession(sessionName, productKey).getProductKeysStruct().classKey;
2702            ChannelKey classChannelKey = new ChannelKey(ChannelType.CB_RECAP_BY_CLASS, new SessionKeyContainer(sessionName, classKey));
2703            CMIRecapConsumer recapConsumer = cmiConsumerCacheFactory.getRecapConsumerCache().getRecapConsumer(sessionName, classKey);
2704 
2705            if (clientListener != null)
2706            {
2707                eventChannel.addChannelListener(eventChannel,clientListener,productChannelKey);
2708            }
2709 
2710 
2711            if (SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().subscribe(classChannelKey, null, recapConsumer) == 1) {
2712                GUILoggerHome.find().debug(TRANSLATOR_NAME+": subscribeRecapForProduct", GUILoggerBusinessProperty.MARKET_QUERY,"subscribing translator to CAS for Recap for session='"+sessionName+"' productKey="+productKey);
2713                try
2714                {
2715                    marketQuery.subscribeRecapForClass(sessionName, classKey, recapConsumer);
2716                }
2717                catch (SystemException e)
2718                {
2719                    SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().unsubscribe(classChannelKey, null, recapConsumer);
2720                    if (clientListener != null)
2721                    {
2722                        eventChannel.removeChannelListener(eventChannel,clientListener,productChannelKey);
2723                    }
2724                    throw e;
2725                }
2726                catch (CommunicationException e)
2727                {
2728                    SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().unsubscribe(classChannelKey, null, recapConsumer);
2729                    if (clientListener != null)
2730                    {
2731                        eventChannel.removeChannelListener(eventChannel,clientListener,productChannelKey);
2732                    }
2733                    throw e;
2734                }
2735                catch (AuthorizationException e)
2736                {
2737                    SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().unsubscribe(classChannelKey, null, recapConsumer);
2738                    if (clientListener != null)
2739                    {
2740                        eventChannel.removeChannelListener(eventChannel,clientListener,productChannelKey);
2741                    }
2742                    throw e;
2743                }
2744                catch (DataValidationException e)
2745                {
2746                    SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().unsubscribe(classChannelKey, null, recapConsumer);
2747                    if (clientListener != null)
2748                    {
2749                        eventChannel.removeChannelListener(eventChannel,clientListener,productChannelKey);
2750                    }
2751                    throw e;
2752                }
2753 
2754            }
2755 
2756        }
2757        catch(NotFoundException e)
2758        {
2759            GUILoggerHome.find().exception(TRANSLATOR_NAME+": subscribeRecapForProduct", "Unable to get SessionProduct. Session:'"+sessionName+"' Key="+productKey, e);
2760        }
2761    }

2820    public void subscribeBookDepth(SessionProduct sessionProduct, EventChannelListener clientListener)
2821            throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException, NotFoundException
2822    {
2823        if (GUILoggerHome.find().isDebugOn() && GUILoggerHome.find().isPropertyOn(GUILoggerBusinessProperty.MARKET_QUERY))
2824        {
2825            Object[] argObj = new Object[3];
2826            argObj[0] = sessionProduct.getTradingSessionName();
2827            argObj[1] = new Integer(sessionProduct.getProductKey());
2828            argObj[2] = clientListener;
2829 
2830            GUILoggerHome.find().debug(TRANSLATOR_NAME+": subscribeBookDepth", GUILoggerBusinessProperty.MARKET_QUERY, argObj);
2831        }
2832 
2833        ChannelKey key = new ChannelKey(ChannelType.CB_BOOK_DEPTH_BY_PRODUCT, new SessionKeyContainer(sessionProduct.getTradingSessionName(), sessionProduct.getProductKey()));
2834 
2835        // For BookDepth by SessionProduct, use the CMIOrderBookConsumer for the SessionProductCLASS.
2836        // Caching a separate consumer per product would create too many consumers.
2837        CMIOrderBookConsumer bookDepthConsumer = cmiConsumerCacheFactory.getBookDepthConsumerCache().getBookDepthConsumer(sessionProduct.getTradingSessionName(),
2838                    sessionProduct.getProductKeysStruct().classKey);
2839 
2840        // translator only subscribe book depth to CAS once, then it caches for multiple book depth subscription for the same product key
2841        int subscribeCount = SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().subscribe(key, clientListener, bookDepthConsumer);
2842        if (subscribeCount == 1)
2843        {
2844            try
2845            {
2846                marketQuery.subscribeBookDepth(sessionProduct.getTradingSessionName(), sessionProduct.getProductKey(), bookDepthConsumer);
2847            }
2848            catch (SystemException e)
2849            {
2850                SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().unsubscribe(key, clientListener, bookDepthConsumer);
2851                throw e;
2852            }
2853            catch (CommunicationException e)
2854            {
2855                SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().unsubscribe(key, clientListener, bookDepthConsumer);
2856                throw e;
2857            }
2858            catch (AuthorizationException e)
2859            {
2860                SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().unsubscribe(key, clientListener, bookDepthConsumer);
2861                throw e;
2862            }
2863            catch (DataValidationException e)
2864            {
2865                SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().unsubscribe(key, clientListener, bookDepthConsumer);
2866                throw e;
2867            }
2868 
2869        }
2870        else // multiple book depth subscriptions for the same product
2871        if (subscribeCount > 1)
2872        {
2873            BookDepthStruct bookDepth = BookDepthCacheFactory.find(sessionProduct.getTradingSessionName()).getBookDepth(new Integer(sessionProduct.getProductKey()));
2874 
2875            ChannelEvent event = EventChannelAdapterFactory.find().getChannelEvent(this, key, bookDepth);
2876            eventChannel.dispatch(event);
2877        }
2878 
2879        if (GUILoggerHome.find().isDebugOn() && GUILoggerHome.find().isPropertyOn(GUILoggerBusinessProperty.MARKET_QUERY))
2880        {
2881            Object[] argObj = new Object[1];
2882            argObj[0] = sessionProduct.getTradingSessionName();
2883            GUILoggerHome.find().debug(TRANSLATOR_NAME+": subscribeBookDepth count = " + subscribeCount, GUILoggerBusinessProperty.MARKET_QUERY, argObj);
2884        }
2885    }

3751            GUILoggerHome.find().debug(TRANSLATOR_NAME+": unsubscribeProductsByClassForSession", GUILoggerBusinessProperty.PRODUCT_QUERY, argObj);
3752        }
3753 
3754        key = new ChannelKey(ChannelType.CB_PRODUCT_UPDATE_BY_CLASS, new SessionKeyContainer(sessionName, classKey));
3755        //int subscriptionCount1 = SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().unsubscribe(key, clientListener, productStatusConsumer);
3756        SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().unsubscribe(key, clientListener, productStatusConsumer);
3757        key = new ChannelKey(ChannelType.CB_PRODUCT_STATE_BY_CLASS, new SessionKeyContainer(sessionName, classKey));
3758        //int subscriptionCount2 = SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().unsubscribe(key, clientListener, productStatusConsumer);
3759        SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().unsubscribe(key, clientListener, productStatusConsumer);
3760        // we're never unsubscribing the translator from the CAS for ProductStatus and Product updates, because it could cause
3761        // problems with the caches getting out of sync.  After the caches are inspected and possibly refactored, this unsubscription
3762        // might be added again.
3763//        if ( subscriptionCount1 == 0 && subscriptionCount2 == 0 )
3764//        {
3765//            tradingSession.unsubscribeProductsByClassForSession(sessionName, classKey, productStatusConsumer);
3766//            CacheClassTrackFactory.find(new SessionKeyContainer(sessionName, classKey)).setSessionProductsLoaded(false);
3767//        }
3768        try {
3769            if ( isStrategy(classKey) ){
3770                unsubscribeStrategiesByClassForSession(sessionName, classKey, clientListener);
3771            }
3772        } catch (NotFoundException e) {
3773            DataValidationException de = new DataValidationException();
3774            de.details = e.details;
3775            throw de;
3776        }
3777    }

3779    public void unsubscribeStrategiesByClassForSession(String sessionName, int classKey, EventChannelListener clientListener)
3780            throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException {
3781 
3782        ChannelKey key = new ChannelKey(ChannelType.CB_STRATEGY_UPDATE, new SessionKeyContainer(sessionName, classKey));
3783        if (GUILoggerHome.find().isDebugOn() && GUILoggerHome.find().isPropertyOn(GUILoggerBusinessProperty.PRODUCT_QUERY))
3784        {
3785            Object[] argObj = new Object[3];
3786            argObj[0] = sessionName;
3787            argObj[1] = new Integer(classKey);
3788            argObj[2] = clientListener;
3789            GUILoggerHome.find().debug(TRANSLATOR_NAME+": unsubscribeStrategiesByClassForSession", GUILoggerBusinessProperty.PRODUCT_QUERY, argObj);
3790        }
3791 
3792        if (SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().unsubscribe(key, clientListener, strategyStatusConsumer) == 0) {
3793        // we're never unsubscribing the translator from the CAS for ProductStatus and Product updates, because it could cause
3794        // problems with the caches getting out of sync.  After the caches are inspected and possibly refactored, this unsubscription
3795        // might be added again.

3797        }

4389    /**
4390     * Accepts a new strategy for addition to the system.
4391     *
4392     * @return the accepted strategy struct
4393     * @param strategyRequest the new strategy request struct
4394     * @exception SystemException
4395     * @exception CommunicationException
4396     * @exception AuthorizationException
4397     * @exception DataValidationException
4398     */
4399    public SessionStrategy acceptSessionStrategy(String sessionName, StrategyRequestStruct strategyRequest)
4400           throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException
4401    {
4402        if (GUILoggerHome.find().isDebugOn() && GUILoggerHome.find().isPropertyOn(GUILoggerBusinessProperty.PRODUCT_DEFINITION))
4403        {
4404            Object[] argObj = new Object[2];
4405            argObj[0] = sessionName;
4406            argObj[1] = strategyRequest;
4407 
4408            GUILoggerHome.find().debug(TRANSLATOR_NAME+": acceptSessionStrategy", GUILoggerBusinessProperty.PRODUCT_DEFINITION, argObj);
4409        }
4410        
4411        // We have to make sure Short Sale and Short Sale Exempt side indicator have been converted to Sell.
4412        // Product Definitions do not contain H and X. 
4413//        for(StrategyLegStruct requestStruct :strategyRequest.strategyLegs)
4414//        {
4415//                if(requestStruct.side == Sides.SELL_SHORT || requestStruct.side == Sides.SELL_SHORT_EXEMPT){
4416//                        requestStruct.side = Sides.SELL;
4417//                }
4418//        }
4419        
4420        SessionStrategyStruct strategy = productDefinition.acceptStrategy(sessionName, strategyRequest);
4421        StrategyStruct strategyStruct = new StrategyStruct();
4422        strategyStruct.product = strategy.sessionProductStruct.productStruct;
4423        strategyStruct.strategyType = strategy.strategyType;
4424        int strategyLength = strategy.sessionStrategyLegs.length;
4425        strategyStruct.strategyLegs = new StrategyLegStruct[strategyLength];
4426        for (int i=0; i<strategyLength; i++) {
4427            strategyStruct.strategyLegs[i] = new StrategyLegStruct();
4428            strategyStruct.strategyLegs[i].product = strategy.sessionStrategyLegs[i].product;
4429            strategyStruct.strategyLegs[i].ratioQuantity = strategy.sessionStrategyLegs[i].ratioQuantity;
4430            strategyStruct.strategyLegs[i].side = strategy.sessionStrategyLegs[i].side;
4431        }
4432        Strategy newStrategy = ProductFactoryHome.find().create(strategyStruct);
4433        ProductQueryCacheFactory.find().addStrategy(newStrategy, strategy.sessionProductStruct.productStruct.productKeys.classKey);
4434        productProcessor.updateStrategy(strategy);
4435        SessionStrategy sessionStrategy = SessionProductFactory.create(strategy);
4436        return sessionStrategy;
4437    }

4479     * @param clientListener  EventChannelListener object to receive trading session
4480     * updates
4481     * @exception SystemException
4482     * @exception CommunicationException
4483     * @exception AuthorizationException
4484     * @exception DataValidationException
4485     */
4486    public void subscribeTradingSessions(EventChannelListener clientListener)
4487           throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException
4488    {
4489        if (GUILoggerHome.find().isDebugOn() && GUILoggerHome.find().isPropertyOn(GUILoggerBusinessProperty.TRADING_SESSION))
4490        {
4491            GUILoggerHome.find().debug(TRANSLATOR_NAME+": subscribeTradingSessions", GUILoggerBusinessProperty.TRADING_SESSION, clientListener);
4492        }
4493 
4494        TradingSessionStruct[] sessions = tradingSessionCache.getCurrentTradingSessions();
4495 
4496        ChannelKey key = new ChannelKey(ChannelType.CB_TRADING_SESSION_STATE, new Integer(0));
4497 
4498        if (SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().subscribe(key, clientListener, tradingSessionStatusConsumer) == 1)        {
4499            try
4500            {
4501                sessions = tradingSession.getCurrentTradingSessions(tradingSessionStatusConsumer);
4502            }
4503            catch (SystemException e)
4504            {
4505                SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().unsubscribe(key, clientListener, tradingSessionStatusConsumer);
4506                throw e;
4507            }
4508            catch (CommunicationException e)
4509            {
4510                SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().unsubscribe(key, clientListener, tradingSessionStatusConsumer);
4511                throw e;
4512            }
4513            catch (AuthorizationException e)
4514            {
4515                SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().unsubscribe(key, clientListener, tradingSessionStatusConsumer);
4516                throw e;
4517            }
4518            catch (DataValidationException e)
4519            {
4520                SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().unsubscribe(key, clientListener, tradingSessionStatusConsumer);
4521                throw e;
4522            }
4523 
4524            tradingSessionCache.addTradingSessions(sessions);
4525        }
4526    }

4813    /**
4814     * Get the most recent CurrentMarket for a session product
4815     */
4816    @SuppressWarnings({"DuplicateThrows"})
4817    public CurrentMarketProductContainer getCurrentMarketSnapshotForProduct(
4818            int timeout, String sessionName, int productKey)
4819            throws AuthorizationException, DataValidationException, NotFoundException,
4820            SystemException, CommunicationException, UserException
4821    {
4822        if(GUILoggerHome.find().isDebugOn() &&
4823           GUILoggerHome.find().isPropertyOn(GUILoggerBusinessProperty.MARKET_QUERY))
4824        {
4825            Object[] argObj = {timeout, sessionName, productKey};
4826            GUILoggerHome.find().debug(TRANSLATOR_NAME + ": getCurrentMarketSnapshotForProduct",
4827                                       GUILoggerBusinessProperty.MARKET_QUERY, argObj);
4828        }
4829 
4830        SessionProduct product = getProductByKeyForSession(sessionName, productKey);
4831        int classKey = product.getProductKeysStruct().classKey;
4832        CurrentMarketV3Cache cmV3Cache = MarketDataCacheFactory.findCurrentMarketV3Cache(sessionName);
4833        CurrentMarketProductContainer retVal;
4834 
4835        // if there wasn't already a subscription for CurrentMarket, get a "snapshot".
4836        if(!cmV3Cache.isSubscribedForClass(classKey))
4837        {
4838            CurrentMarketEventChannelSnapshot listener =
4839                    new CurrentMarketEventChannelSnapshot(timeout, sessionName, productKey);
4840            try
4841            {
4842                retVal = (CurrentMarketProductContainer)listener.getEventChannelData();
4843            }
4844            catch(TimedOutException e)
4845            {
4846                // will throw a TimedOutException if the snapshot didn't get an event from
4847                // the CAS before the predetermined timeout period expired
4848                retVal = new CurrentMarketProductContainerImpl();
4849                // this isn't necessaruly a useful exception to show the user;
4850                // it only means that an event wasn't received within the
4851                //    pre-determined CurrentMarketEventChannelSnapshot.TIME_OUT period
4852                GUILoggerHome.find().exception(e.getMessage(), e);
4853            }
4854        }
4855        else
4856        {
4857            retVal = cmV3Cache.getMarketDataForProduct(classKey, productKey);
4858        }
4859 
4860        return retVal;
4861    }

5254        }
5255        catch(UserException  e)

5257            GUILoggerHome.find().exception(e);
5258        }

5260    }

5262    protected boolean isFirmUser()
5263    {
5264        boolean retVal = false;
5265        Role userRole = getUserRole();
5266 
5267        if (userRole == Role.FIRM || userRole == Role.FIRM_DISPLAY)
5268        {
5269            retVal = true;
5270        }
5271        return retVal;
5272    }
5273 
5274    protected boolean isOrderSubscriptionAllowed()
5275    {
5276        boolean retVal;
5277        Role userRole = getUserRole();
5278 
5279        switch(userRole)
5280        {
5281            case CLASS_DISPLAY:
5282            case EOP:
5283            case DISPLAY_OMT:
5284            case REPORTING:
5285            case OPRA:
5286                retVal = false;
5287                break;
5288            case HELPDESK_OMT:
5289            case BOOTH_OMT:
5290            case CROWD_OMT:
5291            default:
5292                retVal = true;
5293                break;
5294        }
5295 
5296        return retVal;
5297    }

5604        ProductClass productClass = ProductQueryCacheFactory.find().getProductClassByKey(classKey);
5605        if(productClass == null)
5606        {
5607            if (GUILoggerHome.find().isDebugOn() && GUILoggerHome.find().isPropertyOn(GUILoggerBusinessProperty.PRODUCT_QUERY))
5608            {
5609                GUILoggerHome.find().debug(TRANSLATOR_NAME + ": isStrategy calling productQuery.getClassByKey()", GUILoggerBusinessProperty.PRODUCT_QUERY, classKey);
5610            }
5611            ClassStruct classStruct = productQuery.getClassByKey(classKey);
5612 
5613            if (classStruct != null) {
5614                ProductClass rawProductClass = ProductClassFactoryHome.find().create(classStruct);
5615                ProductQueryCacheFactory.find().addClass(rawProductClass, classStruct.productType);
5616                productClass = ProductQueryCacheFactory.find().getProductClassByKey(classKey);
5617            }
5618        }
5619        if (productClass != null) {
5620            if (productClass.getProductType() == ProductTypes.STRATEGY) {
5621                isStrategy = true;
5622            }
5623        }
5624        return isStrategy;
5625    }

5817    /**
5818     * The ChannelKey can be for a ChannelType.CB_USER_MARKET_DATA or ChannelType.CB_USER_MARKET_DATA_BY_PRODUCT, but the
5819     * listeners will only be counted by session/classKey.  The count is maintained so that when all the listeners for a
5820     * class in a particular session have been removed, the UserMarketDataCache will be cleared and unsubscribe from CAS
5821     * event channels for NBBO, Recap, and CurrentMarket for that class.
5822     * added 6/2002
5823     */
5824    private int addUserMarketDataListener(EventChannelListener clientListener, ChannelKey key, String sessionName, int classKey)
5825    {
5826        eventChannel.addChannelListener(EventChannelAdapterFactory.find(), clientListener, key);
5827 
5828        String hashKey = sessionName + classKey;
5829        Integer currentCount;
5830        synchronized(userMarketDataListenerCount)
5831        {
5832            currentCount = userMarketDataListenerCount.get(hashKey);
5833            // increment the count of listeners for this sessionName/class
5834            if(currentCount != null)
5835            {
5836                currentCount = new Integer(currentCount.intValue()+1);
5837            }
5838            else
5839            {
5840                // this is the first listener
5841                currentCount = new Integer(1);
5842            }
5843 
5844            userMarketDataListenerCount.put(hashKey, currentCount);
5845 
5846            GUILoggerHome.find().debug(TRANSLATOR_NAME+": addUserMarketDataListener()",GUILoggerBusinessProperty.MARKET_QUERY,"num InternalEventChannel listeners for session '"+sessionName+"', class "+classKey+" = "+currentCount.intValue());
5847        }
5848        return currentCount.intValue();
5849    }
5850 
5851    /**
5852     * The ChannelKey can be for ChannelType.CB_USER_MARKET_DATA or ChannelType.CB_USER_MARKET_DATA_BY_PRODUCT, but only
5853     * maintaining a count of listeners by session/classKey.  Once all the listeners for a class in a session have been
5854     * removed, the UserMarketDataCache will cleanUp it's caches and unsubscribe for event channels for NBBO, Recap, and
5855     * CurrentMarket updates from the CAS.
5856     * added 6/2002
5857     */
5858    private int removeUserMarketDataListener(EventChannelListener clientListener, ChannelKey key, String sessionName, int classKey)
5859    {
5860        eventChannel.removeChannelListener(EventChannelAdapterFactory.find(), clientListener, key);
5861 
5862        String hashKey = sessionName + classKey;
5863        Integer currentCount;
5864        synchronized(userMarketDataListenerCount)
5865        {
5866            currentCount = userMarketDataListenerCount.get(hashKey);
5867            // do nothing if there are no registered listeners for this session/class
5868            if(currentCount == null || currentCount.intValue() == 0)
5869            {
5870                return 0;
5871            }
5872            // decrement the count of listeners for this sessionName/class
5873            if(currentCount.intValue() > 0)
5874            {
5875                currentCount = new Integer(currentCount.intValue()-1);
5876            }
5877            userMarketDataListenerCount.put(hashKey, currentCount);
5878            // if this was the last USER_MARKET_DATA listener, unsubscribe the UserMarketDataCache
5879            if(currentCount.intValue() == 0)
5880            {
5881                GUILoggerHome.find().debug(TRANSLATOR_NAME+": removeUserMarketDataListener",GUILoggerBusinessProperty.MARKET_QUERY,"No more InternalEventChannel listeners for session '"+sessionName+"', class "+classKey+" -- removing translator interest");
5882                cleanupProductCache(sessionName, classKey);
5883            }
5884            else
5885            {
5886                GUILoggerHome.find().debug(TRANSLATOR_NAME+": removeUserMarketDataListener",GUILoggerBusinessProperty.MARKET_QUERY,"num InternalEventChannel listeners for session '"+sessionName+"', class "+classKey+" = "+currentCount.intValue());
5887            }
5888        }
5889        return currentCount.intValue();
5890    }

5917    public void subscribeBookDepthForClassV2(String sessionName, int classKey, EventChannelListener clientListener)
5918            throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException
5919    {

5921        {
5922            Object[] argObj = new Object[4];
5923            argObj[0] = sessionName;
5924            argObj[1] = new Integer(classKey);
5925            argObj[2] = clientListener;
5926            argObj[3] = new Short(DEFAULT_QUEUE_ACTION);
5927 
5928            GUILoggerHome.find().debug(TRANSLATOR_NAME+": subscribeBookDepthForClassV2", GUILoggerBusinessProperty.MARKET_QUERY, argObj);
5929        }
5930 
5931        ChannelKey key = new ChannelKey(ChannelType.CB_BOOK_DEPTH_BY_CLASS_V2, new SessionKeyContainer(sessionName, classKey));
5932        com.cboe.idl.cmiCallbackV2.CMIOrderBookConsumer orderBookConsumerV2 = cmiConsumerCacheFactoryV2.getBookDepthConsumerCache().getBookDepthConsumer( sessionName, classKey );
5933
