5940            }
5941            catch (SystemException e)
5942            {
5943                SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().unsubscribe(key, clientListener, orderBookConsumerV2);
5944                throw e;
5945            }
5946            catch (CommunicationException e)
5947            {
5948                SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().unsubscribe(key, clientListener, orderBookConsumerV2);
5949                throw e;
5950            }
5951            catch (AuthorizationException e)
5952            {
5953                SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().unsubscribe(key, clientListener, orderBookConsumerV2);
5954                throw e;
5955            }
5956            catch (DataValidationException e)
5957            {
5958                SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().unsubscribe(key, clientListener, orderBookConsumerV2);
5959                throw e;
5960            }
5961        }

5964    public void subscribeBookDepthForProductV2(String sessionName, int productKey, EventChannelListener clientListener)
5965            throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException
5966    {
5967        if (GUILoggerHome.find().isDebugOn() && GUILoggerHome.find().isPropertyOn(GUILoggerBusinessProperty.MARKET_QUERY))
5968        {
5969            Object[] argObj = new Object[4];
5970            argObj[0] = sessionName;
5971            argObj[1] = new Integer(productKey);
5972            argObj[2] = clientListener;
5973            argObj[3] = new Short(DEFAULT_QUEUE_ACTION);
5974 
5975            GUILoggerHome.find().debug(TRANSLATOR_NAME+": subscribeBookDepthForProductV2", GUILoggerBusinessProperty.MARKET_QUERY, argObj);
5976        }
5977 
5978        ChannelKey key = new ChannelKey(ChannelType.CB_BOOK_DEPTH_BY_PRODUCT_V2, new SessionKeyContainer(sessionName, productKey));
5979 
5980        try
5981        {
5982            // for BookDepth by SessionProduct, use the CMIOrderBookConsumer for the SessionProductClass
5983            int classKey = getProductByKeyForSession(sessionName, productKey).getProductKeysStruct().classKey;
5984 
5985            // For BookDepth by SessionProduct, use the CMIOrderBookConsumer for the SessionProductCLASS.
5986            // Caching a separate consumer per product would create too many consumers.
5987            com.cboe.idl.cmiCallbackV2.CMIOrderBookConsumer orderBookConsumerV2 = cmiConsumerCacheFactoryV2.getBookDepthConsumerCache().getBookDepthConsumer( sessionName, classKey );
5988 
5989            // translator only subscribe book depth to CAS once, then it caches for multiple book depth subscription for the same product key
5990            int subscribeCount = SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().subscribe(key, clientListener, orderBookConsumerV2 );
5991            if (subscribeCount == 1)
5992            {
5993                GUILoggerHome.find().debug(TRANSLATOR_NAME+": subscribeBookDepthForProductV2", GUILoggerBusinessProperty.MARKET_QUERY,"subscribing translator to CAS for BookDepth for session='"+sessionName+"' productKey="+productKey);
5994                try
5995                {
5996                    marketQueryV2.subscribeBookDepthForProductV2(sessionName, productKey, orderBookConsumerV2, DEFAULT_QUEUE_ACTION);
5997                }
5998                catch (SystemException e)
5999                {

6389                {

6393            }

6395            {
6396                if(clientListener != null)
6397                {
6398                    eventChannel.removeChannelListener(eventChannel, clientListener, key);
6399                }
6400                throw e;

6409            }
6410        }

7142    public void subscribeCurrentMarketForClassV3(String session, int classKey, EventChannelListener clientListener)
7143            throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException
7144    {
7145        if (GUILoggerHome.find().isDebugOn() && GUILoggerHome.find().isPropertyOn(GUILoggerBusinessProperty.MARKET_QUERY))
7146        {
7147            Object[] argObj = new Object[4];
7148            argObj[0] = session;
7149            argObj[1] = classKey;
7150            argObj[2] = clientListener;
7151            argObj[3] = DEFAULT_QUEUE_ACTION;
7152            GUILoggerHome.find().debug(TRANSLATOR_NAME+": subscribeCurrentMarketForClassV3", GUILoggerBusinessProperty.MARKET_QUERY, argObj);
7153        }
7154 
7155        ChannelKey key = new ChannelKey(ChannelType.CB_CURRENT_MARKET_BY_CLASS_V3, new SessionKeyContainer(session, classKey));
7156        com.cboe.idl.cmiCallbackV3.CMICurrentMarketConsumer currentMarketConsumerV3 = cmiConsumerCacheFactoryV3.getCurrentMarketConsumerCache().getCurrentMarketConsumer(session, classKey);
7157 
7158        if (SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().subscribe(key, clientListener, currentMarketConsumerV3) == 1)
7159        {
7160            GUILoggerHome.find().debug(TRANSLATOR_NAME+": subscribeCurrentMarketForClassV3", GUILoggerBusinessProperty.MARKET_QUERY,"subscribing translator to CAS for CurrentMarket for session='"+session+"' classKey="+classKey);
7161            try
7162            {
7163                MarketDataCacheFactory.findCurrentMarketV3Cache(session).subscribeMarketData(classKey);
7164                marketQueryV3.subscribeCurrentMarketForClassV3(session, classKey, currentMarketConsumerV3, DEFAULT_QUEUE_ACTION);
7165            }
7166            catch (SystemException e)
7167            {
7168                SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().unsubscribe(key, clientListener, currentMarketConsumerV3);
7169                MarketDataCacheFactory.findCurrentMarketV3Cache(session).unsubscribeMarketData(classKey);
7170                throw e;
7171            }
7172            catch (CommunicationException e)
7173            {
7174                SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().unsubscribe(key, clientListener, currentMarketConsumerV3);
7175                MarketDataCacheFactory.findCurrentMarketV3Cache(session).unsubscribeMarketData(classKey);
7176                throw e;
7177            }
7178            catch (AuthorizationException e)
7179            {
7180                SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().unsubscribe(key, clientListener, currentMarketConsumerV3);
7181                MarketDataCacheFactory.findCurrentMarketV3Cache(session).unsubscribeMarketData(classKey);
7182                throw e;
7183            }
7184            catch (DataValidationException e)
7185            {
7186                SubscriptionManagerFactory.find().unsubscribe(key, clientListener, currentMarketConsumerV3);
7187                MarketDataCacheFactory.findCurrentMarketV3Cache(session).unsubscribeMarketData(classKey);
7188                throw e;
7189            }
7190        }
7191        else
7192        {

7579    /**
7580     * This method steps through the array of AuctionSubscriptionResultStruct checking the errocodes and
7581     * generates a DataValidationException if an error is found.  Any none zero errorcode is consider an error...
7582     *
7583     * @param results ArrayList<AuctionSubscriptionResultStruct[]>
7584     */
7585    protected void checkAuctionSubscriptionResults(ArrayList<AuctionSubscriptionResultStruct[]> results) throws DataValidationException
7586    {
7587        boolean error = false;
7588        StringBuffer buffer = new StringBuffer();
7589        for (AuctionSubscriptionResultStruct[] theResult: results)
7590        {
7591            if (theResult[0] != null && theResult[0].subscriptionResult.errorCode != 0)
7592            {
7593                error = true;
7594                buffer.append(FormatFactory.getAuctionSubscriptionResultFormatStrategy().format(theResult[0]));
7595                buffer.append("\n");
7596            }
7597        }
7598 
7599        if (error)
7600        {
7601            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(buffer.toString(), DataValidationCodes.INVALID_AUCTION_TYPE);
7602        }
7603    }

7605    public InternalizationOrderResultStruct acceptInternalizationOrder(OrderEntryStruct primaryOrderEntry,
7606                                                                       OrderEntryStruct matchedOrderEntry,
7607                                                                       short matchOrderType)
7608            throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException,
7609                   NotAcceptedException, TransactionFailedException
7610    {
7611        String methodName = "acceptInternalizationOrder";
7612        logTransaction(methodName, primaryOrderEntry, matchedOrderEntry, MatchOrderTypes.toString(matchOrderType));
7613        InternalizationOrderResultStruct results = null;
7614        try
7615        {
7616            results = orderEntryV3.acceptInternalizationOrder(primaryOrderEntry, matchedOrderEntry, matchOrderType);
7617            checkInternalizationOrderResults(results);

7620        {
7621            try
7622            {
7623                handleTransactionException(methodName, e);
7624            }
7625            catch (AlreadyExistsException ae)
7626            {
7627                // Not valid for this method, must be handled
7628            }
7629        }
7630        return results;
7631    }

7644            Object[] argObj = new Object[5];
7645            argObj[0] = primaryOrder;
7646            argObj[1] = primaryOrderLegDetails;
7647            argObj[2] = matchedOrder;
7648            argObj[3] = matchOrderLegDetails;
7649            argObj[4] = MatchOrderTypes.toString(matchOrderType);
7650 
7651            GUILoggerHome.find().debug(TRANSLATOR_NAME+": acceptInternalizationStrategyOrder", GUILoggerBusinessProperty.ORDER_ENTRY, argObj);
7652        }
7653 
7654        InternalizationOrderResultStruct results = orderEntryV5.acceptInternalizationStrategyOrder(primaryOrder,primaryOrderLegDetails, matchedOrder, matchOrderLegDetails, matchOrderType);
7655        checkInternalizationOrderResults(results);
7656 
7657        return results;
7658    }

7687    private void checkInternalizationOrderResults(InternalizationOrderResultStruct results) throws DataValidationException
7688    {
7689        if (results != null && results.primaryOrderResult != null && results.matchOrderResult != null)
7690        {
7691            if (results.primaryOrderResult.result.errorCode != 0 || results.matchOrderResult.result.errorCode != 0)
7692            {
7693                OperationResultFormatStrategy formatter = FormatFactory.getOperationResultFormatStrategy();
7694 
7695                StringBuffer textBuffer = new StringBuffer(255);
7696                if (results.primaryOrderResult.result.errorCode != 0)
7697                {
7698                     textBuffer.append("Primary: ");
7699                     textBuffer.append(formatter.format(results.primaryOrderResult.result));
7700                     textBuffer.append('\n');
7701                }
7702 
7703                if (results.matchOrderResult.result.errorCode != 0)
7704                {
7705                    textBuffer.append("Match: ");
7706                    textBuffer.append(formatter.format(results.matchOrderResult.result));
7707                }
7708 
7709                throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(textBuffer.toString(), 0);
7710            }
7711        }
7712        else
7713        {
7714            GUILoggerHome.find().alarm("The InternalizationOrderResultStruct is null or internal structs are null...");
7715        }
7716    }

7742    /*
7743     * Logs any ORDER_ENTRY transaction to the audit and debug logs; transaction may have any number of parameters.
7744     */
7745    static void logTransaction(String transactionName, Object... parm)
7746    {
7747        String text = TRANSLATOR_NAME + ": " + transactionName;
7748        GUILoggerHome.find().audit(text, parm);
7749 
7750        if(GUILoggerHome.find().isDebugOn() &&
7751           GUILoggerHome.find().isPropertyOn(GUILoggerBusinessProperty.ORDER_ENTRY))
7752        {
7753            GUILoggerHome.find().debug(text, GUILoggerBusinessProperty.ORDER_ENTRY, parm);
7754        }
7755    }
7756 
7757    static void handleTransactionException(String apiMethodName, Exception e) throws
7758            SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException,
7759            NotAcceptedException, TransactionFailedException, AlreadyExistsException
7760    {
7761        if(e instanceof UserException)
7762        {
7763            StringBuilder buffer = new StringBuilder(apiMethodName).append(" threw CORBA Exception: ")
7764                    .append(e.getMessage()).append(" Details: ");
7765            if(e instanceof SystemException)
7766            {
7767                SystemException se = (SystemException) e;
7768                buffer.append(se.details.message);
7769                GUILoggerHome.find().audit(buffer.toString());
7770                throw se;
7771            }
7772            else if(e instanceof CommunicationException)
7773            {
7774                CommunicationException ce = (CommunicationException) e;
7775                buffer.append(ce.details.message);
7776                GUILoggerHome.find().audit(buffer.toString());
7777                throw ce;
7778            }
7779            else if(e instanceof DataValidationException)
7780            {
7781                DataValidationException dve = (DataValidationException) e;
7782                buffer.append(dve.details.message);
7783                GUILoggerHome.find().audit(buffer.toString());
7784                throw dve;
7785            }
7786            else if(e instanceof TransactionFailedException)
7787            {
7788                TransactionFailedException tfe = (TransactionFailedException) e;
7789                buffer.append(tfe.details.message);
7790                GUILoggerHome.find().audit(buffer.toString());
7791                throw tfe;
7792            }
7793            else if(e instanceof NotAcceptedException)
7794            {
7795                NotAcceptedException nae = (NotAcceptedException) e;
7796                buffer.append(nae.details.message);
7797                GUILoggerHome.find().audit(buffer.toString());
7798                throw nae;
7799            }
7800            else if(e instanceof AuthorizationException)
7801            {
7802                AuthorizationException ae = (AuthorizationException) e;
7803                buffer.append(ae.details.message);
7804                GUILoggerHome.find().audit(buffer.toString());
7805                throw ae;
7806            }
7807            else if(e instanceof AlreadyExistsException)
7808            {
7809                AlreadyExistsException aee = (AlreadyExistsException) e;
7810                buffer.append(aee.details.message);
7811                GUILoggerHome.find().audit(buffer.toString());
7812                throw aee;
7813            }
7814            else
7815            {
7816                GUILoggerHome.find().audit(buffer.toString());
7817                throw new SystemException(buffer.toString(), new ExceptionDetails(buffer.toString(), new Date().toString(), (short)0, 0));
7818            }
7819        }
7820        // this will handle org.omg.CORBA.UNKNOWN, etc.
7821        else
7822        {
7823            String text = apiMethodName + " threw unexpected exception: '"+e.toString()+"' Message: '" + e.getMessage()+"'";
7824            GUILoggerHome.find().audit(text);
7825            // log the original exception
7826            GUILoggerHome.find().exception(e);
7827            throw new SystemException(e.toString(), new ExceptionDetails(text, new Date().toString(), (short) 0, 0));
7828        }
7829    }

7836                matrix.isAllowed(Permission.ORDER_MANAGEMENT_TERMINAL_ACCESS));
7837    }

7846                                            throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException, NotAcceptedException, TransactionFailedException, AlreadyExistsException
7847    {

7859                }
7860                return results;
7861    }
